-- 8월 2일 오전에 생성한 익스포트 파일임
-- 안전하게 메모장 말고 노트패드로 복사한 후 sql문에 붙여넣어 전체 실행할 것
-- 실행 시 drop 테이블과 view에 값을 insert하는 부분에 당연히 에러가 뜨기 때문에 당황하지 않도록 한다.
-- 임포트 시 해당 db의 사용자를 동일하게 하야한다. (nyngw, nyngw)
--------------------------------------------------------

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View DALVIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."DALVIEW" ("DALVIEW_NUMBER", "DALVIEW_DATE", "DALVIEW_ATTEND_TIME", "DALVIEW_OFF_TIME", "DALVIEW_CONTENT", "DALVIEW_MEM_NUMBER", "DALVIEW_SF_NUMBER") AS 
  select dal_number,
      to_char(dal_date,'YY"년"MM"월"DD"일"'),
      to_char(dal_attend_time,'HH24"시"MI"분"SS"초"'),
      to_char(dal_off_time,'HH24"시"MI"분"SS"초"'),
      dal_content,
      dal_mem_number,
      dal_sf_number 
from Diligence_And_Laziness;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View DEPT_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."DEPT_VIEW" ("DEPT_NUMBER", "DEPT_NAME", "DEPT_MEMBERNUMBER", "DEPT_TEL", "DEPT_LEVEL", "DEPT_ADDR", "DEPT_PARENTS", "MEM_NUMBER", "MEM_NAME", "MEM_POSITION_NUMBER", "POSITION_NUMBER", "POSITION_NAME", "POSITION_LEVEL") AS 
  select 
  dept_number,
  dept_name,
  dept_membernumber,
  dept_tel,
  dept_level,
  dept_addr,
  dept_parents,
  mem_number,
  mem_name,
  mem_position_number,
  position_number,
  position_name,
  position_level
from department inner join member on (dept_membernumber=mem_number)
                inner join position on (mem_position_number = position_number);
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View DOCUMENTVIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."DOCUMENTVIEW" ("DV_CODE_NAME", "DV_DOC_DATE", "DV_DOC_NAME", "DV_DOC_NUMBER", "DV_MEM_NAME", "DV_DOC_EADOC") AS 
  select 
      c.code_name, to_char(d.doc_date,'YY"년"MM"월"DD"일"'),d.doc_name,d.doc_number,m.mem_name,d.doc_eadoc
    from  common_code c, document d, member m
    where d.DOC_CODE_NUMBER = c.CODE_NUMBER
    and   d.DOC_MEM_NUMBER = m.mem_number;
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View MEETINGCAL_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."MEETINGCAL_VIEW" ("MT_NUMBER", "RV_DATE", "MD_NAME", "MR_NAME", "MT_READER") AS 
  select 
  mt_number,
  rv_date,
  md_name,
  mr_name,
  mt_reader
from meeting inner join reservation on (mt_rv_number = rv_number)
            inner join meeting_document on (mt_md_number = md_number)
            inner join meetingroom on (mr_number = rv_mr_number);
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View MEMBER_PAY_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."MEMBER_PAY_VIEW" ("MP_NUMBER", "MP_MEM_NUMBER", "MP_BASIC_PAY", "MP_BONUS", "MP_INSURANCE", "MP_FINAL_SALARY", "MP_PAY_DATE", "MEM_NUMBER", "MEM_NAME", "MEM_DEPT_NUMBER", "MEM_POSITION_NUMBER", "DEPT_NUMBER", "DEPT_NAME", "POSITION_NUMBER", "POSITION_NAME") AS 
  select 
  mp_number,
  mp_mem_number,
  mp_basic_pay,
  mp_bonus,
  mp_insurance,
  mp_final_salary,
  to_char(mp_pay_date,'yy/mm/dd') as mp_pay_date,
  mem_number,
  mem_name,
  mem_dept_number,
  mem_position_number,
  dept_number,
  dept_name,
  position_number,
  position_name
from member inner join MEMBER_PAY on (mem_number = mp_mem_number)
            inner join DEPARTMENT on (mem_dept_number = dept_number)
            inner join POSITION on (mem_position_number = position_number);
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View MEMBER_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."MEMBER_VIEW" ("MEM_ID", "MEM_NAME", "MEM_DEPT_NUMBER", "MEM_NUMBER", "DEPT_NAME", "MEM_POSITION_NUMBER", "POSITION_NAME") AS 
  select 
  mem_id,
  mem_name,
  mem_dept_number,
  mem_number,
  dept_name,
  mem_position_number,
  position_name
  
from member  
inner join department on(mem_dept_number=dept_number)
inner join position on(mem_position_number=position_number);
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for View PAY_POLICY_VIEW
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FORCE VIEW "NYNGW"."PAY_POLICY_VIEW" ("PP_NUMBER", "PP_PAY", "PP_POSITION_NUMBER", "PP_WT_NUMBER", "PK_NUMBER", "PK_NAME", "PK_TAX", "POSITION_NUMBER", "POSITION_NAME", "POSITION_LEVEL", "WT_NUMBER", "WT_NAME") AS 
  select 
  pp_number,
  pp_pay,
  pp_position_number,
  pp_wt_number,
  pp_pk_number
  pk_number,
  pk_name,
  pk_tax,
  position_number,
  position_name,
  position_level,
  wt_number,
  wt_name
from pay_policy inner join position on (pp_position_number = position_number)
                inner join pay_kind on (pp_pk_number = pk_number)
                inner join work_time on (pp_wt_number = wt_number);

--  DDL for Table APPROVAL_HISTORY
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE TABLE "NYNGW"."APPROVAL_HISTORY" 
   (	"AH_NUMBER" VARCHAR2(50 BYTE), 
	"AH_CODE_NUMBER" VARCHAR2(50 BYTE), 
	"AH_AST_NUMBER" VARCHAR2(50 BYTE), 
	"AH_EA_NUMBER" VARCHAR2(50 BYTE), 
	"AH_COMMENT" VARCHAR2(1000 BYTE), 
	"AH_TIME" DATE, 
	"AH_STATUS" VARCHAR2(20 BYTE)
   ) SEGMENT CREATION IMMEDIATE 
  PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 40 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING
  STORAGE(INITIAL 65536 NEXT 1048576 MINEXTENTS 1 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645
  PCTINCREASE 0 FREELISTS 1 FREELIST GROUPS 1 BUFFER_POOL DEFAULT FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT CELL_FLASH_CACHE DEFAULT)
  TABLESPACE "SYSTEM" ;

--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Function FN_GETDALCNT
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION "NYNGW"."FN_GETDALCNT" (
P_START IN VARCHAR2, P_END IN VARCHAR2, P_DEPT IN VARCHAR2, P_DAL_NUM IN VARCHAR2)
  RETURN INTEGER
IS
  V_CNT INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_CNT
  FROM   DILIGENCE_AND_LAZINESS D, MEMBER M
  WHERE  D.DAL_MEM_NUMBER = M.MEM_NUMBER
  AND    D.DAL_DATE BETWEEN  TO_DATE(P_START) AND TO_DATE(P_END)+0.99999
  AND    M.MEM_DEPT_NUMBER = P_DEPT
  and    D.DAL_SF_NUMBER = P_DAL_NUM;
 RETURN V_CNT;
  EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
      DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERR : ' || SQLERRM);
    
END;

/
--------------------------------------------------------
--  DDL for Function FN_GETVACATIONCNT
--------------------------------------------------------

  CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION "NYNGW"."FN_GETVACATIONCNT" ( vp_kind_mp IN VARCHAR2 )
  RETURN INTEGER
IS
  V_CNT INTEGER;
BEGIN
  SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_CNT
  FROM DEPARTMENT D, VACATION V,VACATION_POLICY VP,member M
  where D.dept_number=M.mem_dept_number
  and M.mem_number=V.vacation_mem_number
  and VP.VP_NUMBER=V.vacation_VP_NUMBER
  and  VP.VP_KIND  like '%'||vp_kind_mp||'%';
  RETURN V_CNT;
   EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
      DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERR : ' || SQLERRM);
END;

/
